I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
minifier: inlining variables in object when string key is encountered
i noticed a bug with logic used to inline variables, that is present only when object with property of type string is present before variable that should be inlined

```ts
var o = "test-b", l = {
	"test-a": "test-a",
	testb: o,
};
export { l };
/// out
var o = "test-b", l = {
	"test-a": "test-a",
	testb: o
};
export { l };
```
[play](https://playground.oxc.rs/?options=%7B%22run%22%3A%7B%22lint%22%3Atrue%2C%22formatter%22%3Afalse%2C%22transform%22%3Afalse%2C%22isolatedDeclarations%22%3Afalse%2C%22whitespace%22%3Afalse%2C%22mangle%22%3Afalse%2C%22compress%22%3Atrue%2C%22scope%22%3Atrue%2C%22symbol%22%3Atrue%2C%22cfg%22%3Afalse%7D%2C%22parser%22%3A%7B%22extension%22%3A%22tsx%22%2C%22allowReturnOutsideFunction%22%3Atrue%2C%22preserveParens%22%3Atrue%2C%22allowV8Intrinsics%22%3Atrue%2C%22semanticErrors%22%3Atrue%7D%2C%22linter%22%3A%7B%7D%2C%22formatter%22%3A%7B%22useTabs%22%3Afalse%2C%22tabWidth%22%3A2%2C%22endOfLine%22%3A%22lf%22%2C%22printWidth%22%3A80%2C%22singleQuote%22%3Afalse%2C%22jsxSingleQuote%22%3Afalse%2C%22quoteProps%22%3A%22as-needed%22%2C%22trailingComma%22%3A%22all%22%2C%22semi%22%3Atrue%2C%22arrowParens%22%3A%22always%22%2C%22bracketSpacing%22%3Atrue%2C%22bracketSameLine%22%3Afalse%2C%22objectWrap%22%3A%22preserve%22%2C%22singleAttributePerLine%22%3Afalse%7D%2C%22transformer%22%3A%7B%22target%22%3A%22es2015%22%2C%22useDefineForClassFields%22%3Atrue%2C%22experimentalDecorators%22%3Atrue%2C%22emitDecoratorMetadata%22%3Atrue%7D%2C%22isolatedDeclarations%22%3A%7B%22stripInternal%22%3Afalse%7D%2C%22codegen%22%3A%7B%22normal%22%3Atrue%2C%22jsdoc%22%3Atrue%2C%22annotation%22%3Atrue%2C%22legal%22%3Atrue%7D%2C%22compress%22%3A%7B%7D%2C%22mangle%22%3A%7B%22topLevel%22%3Atrue%2C%22keepNames%22%3Afalse%7D%2C%22controlFlow%22%3A%7B%22verbose%22%3Afalse%7D%2C%22inject%22%3A%7B%22inject%22%3A%7B%7D%7D%2C%22define%22%3A%7B%22define%22%3A%7B%7D%7D%7D&code=var+o+%3D+%22test-b%22%2C+l+%3D+%7B%0A%09%22test-a%22%3A+%22string%22%2C%0A%09testb%3A+o%2C%0A%7D%3B%0Aexport+%7B+l+%7D%3B)

this issue is present only when `"test-a"` string is enoutered and it works correctly when `"` can be removed
```ts
var o = "test-b", l = {
	"testa": "test-a",
	testb: o,
};
export { l };
//// out
var l = {
	testa: "test-a",
	testb: "test-b"
};
export { l };
```

</pr_description>

     2	use oxc_ast::ast::*;
     3	use oxc_semantic::{Scoping, SemanticBuilder};
     4	
     5	use crate::{
     6	    CompressOptions, ReusableTraverseCtx,
     7	    peephole::{Normalize, NormalizeOptions, PeepholeOptimizations},
     8	    state::MinifierState,
     9	};
    10	
    11	pub struct Compressor<'a> {
    12	    allocator: &'a Allocator,
    13	}
    14	
    15	impl<'a> Compressor<'a> {
    16	    pub fn new(allocator: &'a Allocator) -> Self {
    17	        Self { allocator }
    18	    }
    19	
    20	    pub fn build(self, program: &mut Program<'a>, options: CompressOptions) {
    21	        let scoping = SemanticBuilder::new().build(program).semantic.into_scoping();
    22	        self.build_with_scoping(program, scoping, options);
    23	    }
    24	
    25	    /// Returns total number of iterations ran.
    26	    pub fn build_with_scoping(
    27	        self,
    28	        program: &mut Program<'a>,
    29	        scoping: Scoping,
    30	        options: CompressOptions,
    31	    ) -> u8 {
    32	        let max_iterations = options.max_iterations;
    33	        let state = MinifierState::new(program.source_type, options, /* dce */ false);
    34	        let mut ctx = ReusableTraverseCtx::new(state, scoping, self.allocator);
    35	        let normalize_options = NormalizeOptions {
    36	            convert_while_to_fors: true,
    37	            convert_const_to_let: true,
    38	            remove_unnecessary_use_strict: true,
    39	        };
    40	        Normalize::new(normalize_options).build(program, &mut ctx);
    41	        Self::run_in_loop(max_iterations, program, &mut ctx)
    42	    }
    43	
    44	    pub fn dead_code_elimination(self, program: &mut Program<'a>, options: CompressOptions) -> u8 {
    45	        let scoping = SemanticBuilder::new().build(program).semantic.into_scoping();
    46	        self.dead_code_elimination_with_scoping(program, scoping, options)
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    /// Returns total number of iterations ran.
    50	    pub fn dead_code_elimination_with_scoping(
    51	        self,
    52	        program: &mut Program<'a>,
    53	        scoping: Scoping,
    54	        options: CompressOptions,
    55	    ) -> u8 {
    56	        let max_iterations = options.max_iterations;
    57	        let state = MinifierState::new(program.source_type, options, /* dce */ true);
    58	        let mut ctx = ReusableTraverseCtx::new(state, scoping, self.allocator);
    59	        let normalize_options = NormalizeOptions {
    60	            convert_while_to_fors: false,
    61	            convert_const_to_let: false,
    62	            remove_unnecessary_use_strict: false,
    63	        };
    64	        Normalize::new(normalize_options).build(program, &mut ctx);
    65	        Self::run_in_loop(max_iterations, program, &mut ctx)
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    /// Fixed-point iteration loop for peephole optimizations.
    69	    fn run_in_loop(
    70	        max_iterations: Option<u8>,
    71	        program: &mut Program<'a>,
    72	        ctx: &mut ReusableTraverseCtx<'a>,
    73	    ) -> u8 {
    74	        let mut iteration = 0u8;
    75	        loop {
    76	            PeepholeOptimizations.run_once(program, ctx);
    77	            if !ctx.state().changed {
    78	                break;
    79	            }
    80	            if let Some(max) = max_iterations {
    81	                if iteration >= max {
    82	                    break;
    83	                }
    84	            } else if iteration > 10 {
    85	                debug_assert!(false, "Ran loop more than 10 times.");
    86	                break;
    87	            }
    88	            iteration += 1;
    89	        }
    90	        iteration
    91	    }
    92	}

     1	use crate::generated::ancestor::Ancestor;
     2	use oxc_ast::ast::*;
     3	use oxc_ecmascript::constant_evaluation::{ConstantEvaluation, ConstantValue};
     4	use oxc_span::GetSpan;
     5	
     6	use crate::TraverseCtx;
     7	
     8	use super::PeepholeOptimizations;
     9	
    10	impl<'a> PeepholeOptimizations {
    11	    pub fn init_symbol_value(decl: &VariableDeclarator<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
    12	        let BindingPattern::BindingIdentifier(ident) = &decl.id else { return };
    13	        let Some(symbol_id) = ident.symbol_id.get() else { return };
    14	        let value = if decl.kind.is_var() || Self::is_for_statement_init(ctx) {
    15	            // - Skip constant value inlining for `var` declarations, due to TDZ problems.
    16	            // - Set None for for statement initializers as the value of these are set by the for statement.
    17	            None
    18	        } else {
    19	            decl.init.as_ref().map_or(Some(ConstantValue::Undefined), |e| e.evaluate_value(ctx))
    20	        };
    21	        ctx.init_value(symbol_id, value);
    22	    }
    23	
    24	    fn is_for_statement_init(ctx: &TraverseCtx<'a>) -> bool {
    25	        ctx.ancestors().nth(1).is_some_and(Ancestor::is_parent_of_for_statement_left)
    26	    }
    27	
    28	    pub fn inline_identifier_reference(expr: &mut Expression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
    29	        let Expression::Identifier(ident) = expr else { return };
    30	        let reference_id = ident.reference_id();
    31	        let Some(symbol_id) = ctx.scoping().get_reference(reference_id).symbol_id() else { return };
    32	        let Some(symbol_value) = ctx.state.symbol_values.get_symbol_value(symbol_id) else {
    33	            return;
    34	        };
    35	        // Skip if there are write references.
    36	        if symbol_value.write_references_count > 0 {
    37	            return;
    38	        }
    39	        let Some(cv) = &symbol_value.initialized_constant else { return };
    40	        if symbol_value.read_references_count == 1
    41	            || match cv {
    42	                ConstantValue::Number(n) => n.fract() == 0.0 && *n >= -99.0 && *n <= 999.0,
    43	                ConstantValue::BigInt(_) => false,
    44	                ConstantValue::String(s) => s.len() <= 3,
    45	                ConstantValue::Boolean(_) | ConstantValue::Undefined | ConstantValue::Null => true,
    46	            }
    47	        {
    48	            *expr = ctx.value_to_expr(expr.span(), cv.clone());
    49	            ctx.state.changed = true;
    50	        }
    51	    }
    52	}
    53

    31	/// Stateless peephole optimizer. The `dce` flag and `changed` state are stored in `MinifierState`.
    32	pub struct PeepholeOptimizations;
    33	
    34	impl<'a> PeepholeOptimizations {
    35	    pub fn run_once(&mut self, program: &mut Program<'a>, ctx: &mut ReusableTraverseCtx<'a>) {
    36	        traverse_mut_with_ctx(self, program, ctx);
    37	    }
    38	
    39	    pub fn commutative_pair<'x, A, F, G, RetF: 'x, RetG: 'x>(
    40	        pair: (&'x A, &'x A),
    41	        check_a: F,
    42	        check_b: G,
    43	    ) -> Option<(RetF, RetG)>
    44	    where
    45	        F: Fn(&'x A) -> Option<RetF>,
    46	        G: Fn(&'x A) -> Option<RetG>,
    47	    {
    48	        match check_a(pair.0) {
    49	            Some(a) => {
    50	                if let Some(b) = check_b(pair.1) {
    51	                    return Some((a, b));
    52	                }
    53	            }
    54	            _ => {
    55	                if let Some(a) = check_a(pair.1)
    56	                    && let Some(b) = check_b(pair.0)
    57	                {
    58	                    return Some((a, b));
    59	                }
    60	            }
    61	        }
    62	        None
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    /// Checks if a member expression's base object may be mutated.
    66	    ///
    67	    /// This is used to prevent incorrect transformations like:
    68	    /// `x.y || (x = {}, x.y = 3)` → `x.y ||= (x = {}, 3)`
    69	    ///
    70	    /// The `||=` operator evaluates `x.y` (capturing `x`) before the RHS reassigns `x`,
    71	    /// which would change the semantics.
    72	    pub fn member_object_may_be_mutated(
    73	        assignment_target: &AssignmentTarget<'a>,
    74	        ctx: &TraverseCtx<'a>,
    75	    ) -> bool {
    76	        let object = match assignment_target {
    77	            AssignmentTarget::ComputedMemberExpression(member_expr) => &member_expr.object,
    78	            AssignmentTarget::PrivateFieldExpression(member_expr) => &member_expr.object,
    79	            AssignmentTarget::StaticMemberExpression(member_expr) => &member_expr.object,
    80	            _ => return false,
    81	        };
    82	
    83	        Self::is_expression_that_reference_may_change(object, ctx)
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    /// Checks if an expression's reference may change due to mutation.
    87	    ///
    88	    /// Returns `true` if the expression references a symbol that may be mutated,
    89	    /// or if the expression is not a simple identifier/this reference.
    90	    pub fn is_expression_that_reference_may_change(
    91	        expr: &Expression<'a>,
    92	        ctx: &TraverseCtx<'a>,
    93	    ) -> bool {
    94	        match expr {
    95	            Expression::Identifier(id) => {
    96	                if let Some(symbol_id) = ctx.scoping().get_reference(id.reference_id()).symbol_id()
    97	                {
    98	                    ctx.scoping().symbol_is_mutated(symbol_id)
    99	                } else {
   100	                    true
   101	                }
   102	            }
   103	            Expression::ThisExpression(_) => false,
   104	            _ => true,
   105	        }
   106	    }
   107	}
   108	
   109	impl<'a> Traverse<'a> for PeepholeOptimizations {
   110	    fn enter_program(&mut self, _program: &mut Program<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   111	        ctx.state.symbol_values.clear();
   112	        ctx.state.changed = false;
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    fn exit_program(&mut self, program: &mut Program<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   116	        if ctx.state.changed {
   117	            // Remove unused references by visiting the AST again and diff the collected references.
   118	            let refs_before =
   119	                ctx.scoping().resolved_references().flatten().copied().collect::<FxHashSet<_>>();
   120	            let mut counter = ReferencesCounter::default();
   121	            counter.visit_program(program);
   122	            for reference_id_to_remove in refs_before.difference(&counter.refs) {
   123	                ctx.scoping_mut().delete_reference(*reference_id_to_remove);
   124	            }
   125	        }
   126	        // Only check class_symbols_stack in full optimization mode (not DCE mode)
   127	        debug_assert!(ctx.state.dce || ctx.state.class_symbols_stack.is_exhausted());
   128	    }
   129	
   130	    fn exit_statements(&mut self, stmts: &mut Vec<'a, Statement<'a>>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   131	        Self::minimize_statements(stmts, ctx);
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    fn enter_statement(&mut self, stmt: &mut Statement<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   135	        if ctx.state.dce {
   136	            return;
   137	        }
   138	        Self::keep_track_of_pure_functions(stmt, ctx);
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    fn exit_statement(&mut self, stmt: &mut Statement<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   142	        if ctx.state.dce {
   143	            match stmt {
   144	                Statement::BlockStatement(_) => Self::try_optimize_block(stmt, ctx),
   145	                Statement::IfStatement(_) => Self::try_fold_if(stmt, ctx),
   146	                Statement::ForStatement(_) => Self::try_fold_for(stmt, ctx),
   147	                Statement::TryStatement(_) => Self::try_fold_try(stmt, ctx),
   148	                Statement::LabeledStatement(_) => Self::try_fold_labeled(stmt, ctx),
   149	                Statement::FunctionDeclaration(_) => {
   150	                    Self::remove_unused_function_declaration(stmt, ctx);
   151	                }
   152	                Statement::ClassDeclaration(_) => {
   153	                    Self::remove_unused_class_declaration(stmt, ctx);
   154	                }
   155	                Statement::ExpressionStatement(_) => {
   156	                    Self::try_fold_expression_stmt(stmt, ctx);
   157	                }
   158	                Statement::ImportDeclaration(_) => {
   159	                    Self::remove_unused_import_specifiers(stmt, ctx);
   160	                }
   161	                _ => {}
   162	            }
   163	        } else {
   164	            match stmt {
   165	                Statement::BlockStatement(_) => Self::try_optimize_block(stmt, ctx),
   166	                Statement::IfStatement(s) => {
   167	                    Self::minimize_expression_in_boolean_context(&mut s.test, ctx);
   168	                    Self::try_fold_if(stmt, ctx);
   169	                    if let Statement::IfStatement(if_stmt) = stmt
   170	                        && let Some(folded_stmt) = Self::try_minimize_if(if_stmt, ctx)
   171	                    {
   172	                        *stmt = folded_stmt;
   173	                        ctx.state.changed = true;
   174	                    }
   175	                }
   176	                Statement::WhileStatement(s) => {
   177	                    Self::minimize_expression_in_boolean_context(&mut s.test, ctx);
   178	                }
   179	                Statement::ForStatement(s) => {
   180	                    if let Some(test) = &mut s.test {
   181	                        Self::minimize_expression_in_boolean_context(test, ctx);
   182	                    }
   183	                    Self::try_fold_for(stmt, ctx);
   184	                }
   185	                Statement::DoWhileStatement(s) => {
   186	                    Self::minimize_expression_in_boolean_context(&mut s.test, ctx);
   187	                }
   188	                Statement::TryStatement(_) => Self::try_fold_try(stmt, ctx),
   189	                Statement::LabeledStatement(_) => Self::try_fold_labeled(stmt, ctx),
   190	                Statement::FunctionDeclaration(_) => {
   191	                    Self::remove_unused_function_declaration(stmt, ctx);
   192	                }
   193	                Statement::ClassDeclaration(_) => Self::remove_unused_class_declaration(stmt, ctx),
   194	                Statement::ImportDeclaration(_) => Self::remove_unused_import_specifiers(stmt, ctx),
   195	                _ => {}
   196	            }
   197	            Self::try_fold_expression_stmt(stmt, ctx);
   198	        }
   199	    }
   200	
   201	    fn exit_for_statement(&mut self, stmt: &mut ForStatement<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   202	        if ctx.state.dce {
   203	            return;
   204	        }
   205	        Self::substitute_for_statement(stmt, ctx);
   206	        Self::minimize_for_statement(stmt, ctx);
   207	    }
   208	
   209	    fn exit_return_statement(&mut self, stmt: &mut ReturnStatement<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   210	        if ctx.state.dce {
   211	            return;
   212	        }
   213	        Self::substitute_return_statement(stmt, ctx);
   214	    }
   215	
   216	    fn exit_variable_declaration(
   217	        &mut self,
   218	        decl: &mut VariableDeclaration<'a>,
   219	        ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>,
   220	    ) {
   221	        if ctx.state.dce {
   222	            return;
   223	        }

   225	    }
   226	
   227	    fn exit_variable_declarator(
   228	        &mut self,
   229	        decl: &mut VariableDeclarator<'a>,
   230	        ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>,
   231	    ) {
   232	        Self::init_symbol_value(decl, ctx);
   233	    }
   234	
   235	    fn exit_expression(&mut self, expr: &mut Expression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   236	        if ctx.state.dce {
   237	            match expr {
   238	                Expression::TemplateLiteral(t) => {
   239	                    Self::inline_template_literal(t, ctx);
   240	                }
   241	                Expression::ObjectExpression(e) => Self::fold_object_exp(e, ctx),
   242	                Expression::BinaryExpression(_) => {
   243	                    Self::fold_binary_expr(expr, ctx);
   244	                    Self::fold_binary_typeof_comparison(expr, ctx);
   245	                }
   246	                Expression::UnaryExpression(_) => Self::fold_unary_expr(expr, ctx),
   247	                Expression::StaticMemberExpression(_) => {
   248	                    Self::fold_static_member_expr(expr, ctx);
   249	                }
   250	                Expression::ComputedMemberExpression(_) => {
   251	                    Self::fold_computed_member_expr(expr, ctx);
   252	                }
   253	                Expression::LogicalExpression(_) => Self::fold_logical_expr(expr, ctx),
   254	                Expression::ChainExpression(_) => Self::fold_chain_expr(expr, ctx),
   255	                Expression::CallExpression(_) => {
   256	                    Self::fold_call_expression(expr, ctx);
   257	                    Self::substitute_iife_call(expr, ctx);
   258	                    Self::remove_dead_code_call_expression(expr, ctx);
   259	                }
   260	                Expression::ConditionalExpression(_) => {
   261	                    Self::try_fold_conditional_expression(expr, ctx);
   262	                }
   263	                Expression::SequenceExpression(_) => {
   264	                    Self::remove_sequence_expression(expr, ctx);
   265	                }
   266	                Expression::AssignmentExpression(_) => {
   267	                    Self::remove_unused_assignment_expr(expr, ctx);
   268	                }
   269	                _ => {}
   270	            }
   271	        } else {
   272	            match expr {
   273	                Expression::TemplateLiteral(t) => {
   274	                    Self::inline_template_literal(t, ctx);
   275	                    Self::substitute_template_literal(expr, ctx);
   276	                }
   277	                Expression::ObjectExpression(e) => Self::fold_object_exp(e, ctx),
   278	                Expression::BinaryExpression(e) => {
   279	                    Self::substitute_swap_binary_expressions(e);
   280	                    Self::fold_binary_expr(expr, ctx);
   281	                    Self::fold_binary_typeof_comparison(expr, ctx);
   282	                    Self::minimize_loose_boolean(expr, ctx);
   283	                    Self::minimize_binary(expr, ctx);
   284	                    Self::substitute_loose_equals_undefined(expr, ctx);
   285	                    Self::substitute_typeof_undefined(expr, ctx);
   286	                    Self::substitute_rotate_binary_expression(expr, ctx);
   287	                }
   288	                Expression::UnaryExpression(_) => {
   289	                    Self::fold_unary_expr(expr, ctx);
   290	                    Self::minimize_unary(expr, ctx);
   291	                    Self::substitute_unary_plus(expr, ctx);
   292	                }
   293	                Expression::StaticMemberExpression(_) => {
   294	                    Self::fold_static_member_expr(expr, ctx);
   295	                    Self::replace_known_property_access(expr, ctx);
   296	                }
   297	                Expression::ComputedMemberExpression(_) => {
   298	                    Self::fold_computed_member_expr(expr, ctx);
   299	                    Self::replace_known_property_access(expr, ctx);
   300	                }
   301	                Expression::LogicalExpression(_) => {
   302	                    Self::fold_logical_expr(expr, ctx);
   303	                    Self::minimize_logical_expression(expr, ctx);
   304	                    Self::substitute_is_object_and_not_null(expr, ctx);
   305	                    Self::substitute_rotate_logical_expression(expr, ctx);
   306	                }
   307	                Expression::ChainExpression(_) => {
   308	                    Self::fold_chain_expr(expr, ctx);
   309	                    Self::substitute_chain_expression(expr, ctx);
   310	                }
   311	                Expression::CallExpression(_) => {
   312	                    Self::fold_call_expression(expr, ctx);
   313	                    Self::substitute_iife_call(expr, ctx);
   314	                    Self::remove_dead_code_call_expression(expr, ctx);
   315	                    Self::replace_concat_chain(expr, ctx);
   316	                    Self::replace_known_global_methods(expr, ctx);
   317	                    Self::substitute_simple_function_call(expr, ctx);
   318	                    Self::substitute_object_or_array_constructor(expr, ctx);
   319	                }
   320	                Expression::ConditionalExpression(logical_expr) => {
   321	                    Self::minimize_expression_in_boolean_context(&mut logical_expr.test, ctx);
   322	                    if let Some(changed) = Self::minimize_conditional_expression(logical_expr, ctx)
   323	                    {
   324	                        *expr = changed;
   325	                        ctx.state.changed = true;
   326	                    }
   327	                    Self::try_fold_conditional_expression(expr, ctx);
   328	                }
   329	                Expression::AssignmentExpression(e) => {
   330	                    Self::minimize_normal_assignment_to_combined_logical_assignment(e, ctx);
   331	                    Self::minimize_normal_assignment_to_combined_assignment(e, ctx);
   332	                    Self::minimize_assignment_to_update_expression(expr, ctx);
   333	                    Self::remove_unused_assignment_expr(expr, ctx);
   334	                }
   335	                Expression::SequenceExpression(_) => Self::remove_sequence_expression(expr, ctx),
   336	                Expression::ArrowFunctionExpression(e) => Self::substitute_arrow_expression(e, ctx),
   337	                Expression::FunctionExpression(e) => Self::try_remove_name_from_functions(e, ctx),
   338	                Expression::ClassExpression(e) => Self::try_remove_name_from_classes(e, ctx),
   339	                Expression::NewExpression(e) => {
   340	                    Self::substitute_typed_array_constructor(e, ctx);
   341	                    Self::substitute_global_new_expression(expr, ctx);
   342	                    Self::substitute_object_or_array_constructor(expr, ctx);
   343	                }
   344	                Expression::BooleanLiteral(_) => Self::substitute_boolean(expr, ctx),
   345	                Expression::ArrayExpression(_) => Self::substitute_array_expression(expr, ctx),
   346	                Expression::Identifier(_) => Self::inline_identifier_reference(expr, ctx),
   347	                _ => {}
   348	            }
   349	        }
   350	    }
   351	
   352	    fn exit_unary_expression(&mut self, expr: &mut UnaryExpression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   353	        if ctx.state.dce {
   354	            return;
   355	        }
   356	        if expr.operator.is_not() {
   357	            Self::minimize_expression_in_boolean_context(&mut expr.argument, ctx);
   358	        }
   359	    }

   363	            return;
   364	        }

   366	        Self::remove_empty_spread_arguments(&mut e.arguments);
   367	    }

   372	        }

    24	/// A peephole optimization that minimizes code by simplifying conditional
    25	/// expressions, replacing IFs with HOOKs, replacing object constructors
    26	/// with literals, and simplifying returns.
    27	/// <https://github.com/google/closure-compiler/blob/v20240609/src/com/google/javascript/jscomp/PeepholeSubstituteAlternateSyntax.java>
    28	impl<'a> PeepholeOptimizations {
    29	    pub fn substitute_object_property(prop: &mut ObjectProperty<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
    30	        // <https://tc39.es/ecma262/2024/multipage/ecmascript-language-expressions.html#sec-runtime-semantics-propertydefinitionevaluation>
    31	        if !prop.method
    32	            && let PropertyKey::StringLiteral(str) = &prop.key
    33	        {
    34	            // "{ __proto__ }" sets prototype, while "{ ['__proto__'] }" does not
    35	            if str.value == "__proto__" {
    36	                return;
    37	            }
    38	        }
    39	
    40	        Self::try_compress_property_key(&mut prop.key, &mut prop.computed, ctx);
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    pub fn substitute_assignment_target_property_property(
    44	        prop: &mut AssignmentTargetPropertyProperty<'a>,
    45	        ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>,
    46	    ) {
    47	        Self::try_compress_property_key(&mut prop.name, &mut prop.computed, ctx);
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    pub fn substitute_assignment_target_property(
    51	        prop: &mut AssignmentTargetProperty<'a>,
    52	        ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>,
    53	    ) {
    54	        Self::try_compress_assignment_target_property(prop, ctx);
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    pub fn try_compress_assignment_target_property(
    58	        prop: &mut AssignmentTargetProperty<'a>,
    59	        ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>,
    60	    ) {
    61	        // `a: a` -> `a`
    62	        if let AssignmentTargetProperty::AssignmentTargetPropertyProperty(assign_target_prop_prop) =
    63	            prop
    64	        {
    65	            let Some(prop_name) = assign_target_prop_prop.name.static_name() else { return };
    66	            let Some(ident) = assign_target_prop_prop.binding.identifier_mut() else {
    67	                return;
    68	            };
    69	            if prop_name == ident.name {
    70	                *prop = ctx.ast.assignment_target_property_assignment_target_property_identifier(
    71	                    ident.span,
    72	                    ident.take_in(ctx.ast),
    73	                    None,
    74	                );
    75	                ctx.state.changed = true;
    76	            }
    77	        }
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    pub fn substitute_binding_property(prop: &mut BindingProperty<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
    81	        Self::try_compress_property_key(&mut prop.key, &mut prop.computed, ctx);
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    pub fn substitute_method_definition(
    85	        prop: &mut MethodDefinition<'a>,
    86	        ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>,
    87	    ) {
    88	        let property_key_parent: ClassPropertyKeyParent = prop.into();
    89	        // Only check for computed property restrictions if this is actually a computed property
    90	        if prop.computed
    91	            && let PropertyKey::StringLiteral(str) = &prop.key
    92	            && property_key_parent.should_keep_as_computed_property(&str.value)
    93	        {
    94	            return;
    95	        }
    96	        Self::try_compress_property_key(&mut prop.key, &mut prop.computed, ctx);
    97	    }
    98	
    99	    pub fn substitute_property_definition(
   100	        prop: &mut PropertyDefinition<'a>,
   101	        ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>,
   102	    ) {
   103	        let property_key_parent: ClassPropertyKeyParent = prop.into();
   104	        // Only check for computed property restrictions if this is actually a computed property
   105	        if prop.computed
   106	            && let PropertyKey::StringLiteral(str) = &prop.key
   107	            && property_key_parent.should_keep_as_computed_property(&str.value)
   108	        {
   109	            return;
   110	        }
   111	        Self::try_compress_property_key(&mut prop.key, &mut prop.computed, ctx);
   112	    }
   113	
   114	    pub fn substitute_accessor_property(
   115	        prop: &mut AccessorProperty<'a>,
   116	        ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>,
   117	    ) {
   118	        let property_key_parent: ClassPropertyKeyParent = prop.into();
   119	        // Only check for computed property restrictions if this is actually a computed property
   120	        if prop.computed
   121	            && let PropertyKey::StringLiteral(str) = &prop.key
   122	            && property_key_parent.should_keep_as_computed_property(&str.value)
   123	        {
   124	            return;
   125	        }
   126	        Self::try_compress_property_key(&mut prop.key, &mut prop.computed, ctx);
   127	    }
   128	
   129	    pub fn substitute_for_statement(stmt: &mut ForStatement<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   130	        Self::try_rewrite_arguments_copy_loop(stmt, ctx);
   131	    }
   132	
   133	    pub fn substitute_variable_declaration(
   134	        decl: &mut VariableDeclaration<'a>,
   135	        ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>,
   136	    ) {
   137	        for declarator in &mut decl.declarations {
   138	            Self::compress_variable_declarator(declarator, ctx);
   139	        }
   140	    }
   141	
   142	    pub fn substitute_call_expression(expr: &mut CallExpression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   143	        Self::try_flatten_arguments(&mut expr.arguments, ctx);
   144	        Self::try_rewrite_object_callee_indirect_call(expr, ctx);
   145	    }
   146	
   147	    pub fn substitute_new_expression(expr: &mut NewExpression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   148	        Self::try_flatten_arguments(&mut expr.arguments, ctx);
   149	    }
   150	
   151	    pub fn substitute_chain_expression(expr: &mut Expression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   152	        let Expression::ChainExpression(e) = expr else { return };
   153	        Self::try_flatten_nested_chain_expression(e, ctx);
   154	        Self::substitute_chain_call_expression(e, ctx);
   155	    }
   156	
   157	    pub fn substitute_swap_binary_expressions(e: &mut BinaryExpression<'a>) {
   158	        if e.operator.is_equality()
   159	            && (e.left.is_literal() || e.left.is_no_substitution_template() || e.left.is_void_0())
   160	            && !e.right.is_literal()
   161	        {
   162	            std::mem::swap(&mut e.left, &mut e.right);
   163	        }
   164	    }
   165	
   166	    /// `() => { return foo })` -> `() => foo`
   167	    pub fn substitute_arrow_expression(
   168	        arrow_expr: &mut ArrowFunctionExpression<'a>,
   169	        ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>,
   170	    ) {
   171	        if !arrow_expr.expression
   172	            && arrow_expr.body.directives.is_empty()
   173	            && arrow_expr.body.statements.len() == 1
   174	            && let Some(body) = arrow_expr.body.statements.first_mut()
   175	            && let Statement::ReturnStatement(ret_stmt) = body
   176	        {
   177	            let return_stmt_arg = ret_stmt.argument.as_mut().map(|arg| arg.take_in(ctx.ast));
   178	            if let Some(arg) = return_stmt_arg {
   179	                *body = ctx.ast.statement_expression(arg.span(), arg);
   180	                arrow_expr.expression = true;
   181	                ctx.state.changed = true;
   182	            }
   183	        }
   184	    }
   185	
   186	    /// Compress `typeof foo == "undefined"`
   187	    ///
   188	    /// - `typeof foo == "undefined"` (if foo is not resolved) -> `typeof foo > "u"`
   189	    /// - `typeof foo != "undefined"` (if foo is not resolved) -> `typeof foo < "u"`
   190	    /// - `typeof foo == "undefined"` -> `foo === undefined`
   191	    /// - `typeof foo != "undefined"` -> `foo !== undefined`
   192	    /// - `typeof foo.bar == "undefined"` -> `foo.bar === undefined` (for any expression e.g.`typeof (foo + "")`)
   193	    /// - `typeof foo.bar != "undefined"` -> `foo.bar !== undefined` (for any expression e.g.`typeof (foo + "")`)
   194	    ///
   195	    /// Enabled by `compress.typeofs`
   196	    pub fn substitute_typeof_undefined(expr: &mut Expression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   197	        let Expression::BinaryExpression(e) = expr else { return };
   198	        let Expression::UnaryExpression(unary_expr) = &e.left else { return };
   199	        if !unary_expr.operator.is_typeof() {
   200	            return;
   201	        }
   202	        let (new_eq_op, new_comp_op) = match e.operator {
   203	            BinaryOperator::Equality | BinaryOperator::StrictEquality => {
   204	                (BinaryOperator::StrictEquality, BinaryOperator::GreaterThan)
   205	            }
   206	            BinaryOperator::Inequality | BinaryOperator::StrictInequality => {
   207	                (BinaryOperator::StrictInequality, BinaryOperator::LessThan)
   208	            }
   209	            _ => return,
   210	        };
   211	        if !e.right.is_specific_string_literal("undefined") {
   212	            return;
   213	        }
   214	        *expr = if let Expression::Identifier(ident) = &unary_expr.argument
   215	            && ctx.is_global_reference(ident)
   216	        {
   217	            let left = e.left.take_in(ctx.ast);
   218	            let right = ctx.ast.expression_string_literal(e.right.span(), "u", None);
   219	            ctx.ast.expression_binary(e.span, left, new_comp_op, right)
   220	        } else {
   221	            let span = e.span;
   222	            let Expression::UnaryExpression(unary_expr) = &mut e.left else { return };
   223	            ctx.ast.expression_binary(
   224	                span,
   225	                unary_expr.take_in(ctx.ast).argument,
   226	                new_eq_op,
   227	                ctx.ast.void_0(e.right.span()),
   228	            )
   229	        };
   230	        ctx.state.changed = true;
   231	    }
   232	
   233	    /// Remove unary `+` if `ToNumber` conversion is done by the parent expression
   234	    ///
   235	    /// - `1 - +b` => `1 - b` (for other operators as well)
   236	    /// - `+a - 1` => `a - 1` (for other operators as well)
   237	    pub fn substitute_unary_plus(expr: &mut Expression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   238	        let Expression::UnaryExpression(e) = expr else { return };
   239	        if e.operator != UnaryOperator::UnaryPlus {
   240	            return;
   241	        }
   242	        let Some(parent_expression) = ctx.ancestors().next() else { return };
   243	        let parent_expression_does_to_number_conversion = match parent_expression {
   244	            Ancestor::BinaryExpressionLeft(e) => {
   245	                Self::is_binary_operator_that_does_number_conversion(*e.operator())
   246	                    && e.right().value_type(ctx).is_number()
   247	            }
   248	            Ancestor::BinaryExpressionRight(e) => {
   249	                Self::is_binary_operator_that_does_number_conversion(*e.operator())
   250	                    && e.left().value_type(ctx).is_number()
   251	            }
   252	            _ => false,
   253	        };
   254	        if !parent_expression_does_to_number_conversion {
   255	            return;
   256	        }
   257	        *expr = e.argument.take_in(ctx.ast);
   258	        ctx.state.changed = true;
   259	    }
   260	
   261	    /// For `+a - n` => `a - n` (assuming n is a number)
   262	    ///
   263	    /// Before compression the evaluation is:
   264	    /// 1. `a_2 = ToNumber(a)`
   265	    /// 2. `a_3 = ToNumeric(a_2)`
   266	    /// 3. `n_2 = ToNumeric(n)` (no-op since n is a number)
   267	    /// 4. If the type of `a_3` is not number, throw an error
   268	    /// 5. Calculate the result of the binary operation
   269	    ///
   270	    /// After compression, step 1 is removed. The difference we need to care is
   271	    /// the difference with `ToNumber(a)` and `ToNumeric(a)` because `ToNumeric(a_2)` is a no-op.
   272	    ///
   273	    /// - When `a` is an object and `ToPrimitive(a, NUMBER)` returns a BigInt,
   274	    ///   - `ToNumeric(a)` will return that value. But the binary operation will throw an error in step 4.
   275	    ///   - `ToNumber(a)` will throw an error.
   276	    /// - When `a` is an object and `ToPrimitive(a, NUMBER)` returns a value other than BigInt,
   277	    ///   `ToNumeric(a)` and `ToNumber(a)` works the same. Because the step 2 in `ToNumeric` is always `false`.
   278	    /// - When `a` is BigInt,
   279	    ///   - `ToNumeric(a)` will return that value. But the binary operation will throw an error in step 4.
   280	    ///   - `ToNumber(a)` will throw an error.
   281	    /// - When `a` is not a object nor a BigInt, `ToNumeric(a)` and `ToNumber(a)` works the same.
   282	    ///   Because the step 2 in `ToNumeric` is always `false`.
   283	    ///
   284	    /// Thus, removing `+` is fine.
   285	    fn is_binary_operator_that_does_number_conversion(operator: BinaryOperator) -> bool {
   286	        matches!(
   287	            operator,
   288	            BinaryOperator::Exponential
   289	                | BinaryOperator::Multiplication
   290	                | BinaryOperator::Division
   291	                | BinaryOperator::Remainder
   292	                | BinaryOperator::Subtraction
   293	                | BinaryOperator::ShiftLeft
   294	                | BinaryOperator::ShiftRight
   295	                | BinaryOperator::ShiftRightZeroFill
   296	                | BinaryOperator::BitwiseAnd
   297	                | BinaryOperator::BitwiseXOR
   298	                | BinaryOperator::BitwiseOR
   299	        )
   300	    }
   301	
   302	    /// `a || (b || c);` -> `(a || b) || c;`
   303	    pub fn substitute_rotate_logical_expression(
   304	        expr: &mut Expression<'a>,
   305	        ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>,
   306	    ) {
   307	        let Expression::LogicalExpression(e) = expr else { return };
   308	        let Expression::LogicalExpression(right) = &e.right else { return };
   309	        if right.operator != e.operator {
   310	            return;
   311	        }
   312	        let Expression::LogicalExpression(mut right) = e.right.take_in(ctx.ast) else { return };
   313	        let mut new_left = ctx.ast.expression_logical(
   314	            e.span,
   315	            e.left.take_in(ctx.ast),
   316	            e.operator,
   317	            right.left.take_in(ctx.ast),
   318	        );
   319	        Self::substitute_rotate_logical_expression(&mut new_left, ctx);
   320	        *expr =
   321	            ctx.ast.expression_logical(e.span, new_left, e.operator, right.right.take_in(ctx.ast));
   322	        ctx.state.changed = true;
   323	    }
   324	
   325	    /// Rotate associative binary operators:
   326	    /// - `a | (b | c)` -> `(a | b) | c`
   327	    ///
   328	    /// Rotate commutative operators to reduce parentheses:
   329	    /// - `a * (b % c)` -> `b % c * a`
   330	    /// - `a * (b / c)` -> `b / c * a`
   331	    pub fn substitute_rotate_binary_expression(
   332	        expr: &mut Expression<'a>,
   333	        ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>,
   334	    ) {
   335	        let Expression::BinaryExpression(e) = expr else { return };
   336	
   337	        // Handle associative rotation
   338	        let is_associative = matches!(
   339	            e.operator,
   340	            BinaryOperator::BitwiseOR | BinaryOperator::BitwiseAnd | BinaryOperator::BitwiseXOR
   341	        );
   342	        if is_associative
   343	            && let Expression::BinaryExpression(right) = &e.right
   344	            && right.operator == e.operator
   345	            && !right.right.may_have_side_effects(ctx)
   346	        {
   347	            let Expression::BinaryExpression(mut right) = e.right.take_in(ctx.ast) else {
   348	                return;
   349	            };

   351	                e.span,
   352	                e.left.take_in(ctx.ast),
   353	                e.operator,
   354	                right.left.take_in(ctx.ast),
   355	            );

   358	                e.span,
   359	                new_left,

   361	                right.right.take_in(ctx.ast),
   362	            );
   363	            ctx.state.changed = true;
   364	            return;

   367	        // Handle commutative rotation

   369	            && matches!(e.operator, BinaryOperator::Multiplication)
   370	            && e.operator.precedence() == right.operator.precedence()

   382	                && !right.right.may_have_side_effects(ctx)
   383	            {
   384	                let left = e.left.take_in(ctx.ast);
   385	                let right = e.right.take_in(ctx.ast);
   386	                e.right = left;

   978	    /// Fold `Boolean`, ///
   979	    /// `Boolean(a)` -> `!!a`
   980	    /// `Number(0)` -> `0`
   981	    /// `String()` -> `''`
   982	    /// `BigInt(1)` -> `1`
   983	    pub fn substitute_simple_function_call(expr: &mut Expression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   984	        let Expression::CallExpression(e) = expr else { return };
   985	        if e.optional || e.arguments.len() >= 2 {
   986	            return;
   987	        }
   988	        let Expression::Identifier(ident) = &e.callee else { return };
   989	        let name = ident.name.as_str();
   990	        if !matches!(name, "Boolean" | "Number" | "String" | "BigInt") {
   991	            return;
   992	        }
   993	        if !ctx.is_global_reference(ident) {
   994	            return;
   995	        }
   996	        let span = e.span;
   997	        let args = &mut e.arguments;
   998	        let arg = match args.get_mut(0) {
   999	            None => None,
  1000	            Some(arg) => match arg.as_expression_mut() {
  1001	                Some(arg) => Some(arg),
  1002	                None => return,
  1003	            },
  1004	        };
  1005	        let changed = match name {
  1006	            // `Boolean(a)` -> `!!(a)`
  1007	            // http://www.ecma-international.org/ecma-262/6.0/index.html#sec-boolean-constructor-boolean-value
  1008	            // and
  1009	            // http://www.ecma-international.org/ecma-262/6.0/index.html#sec-logical-not-operator-runtime-semantics-evaluation
  1010	            "Boolean" => match arg {
  1011	                None => Some(ctx.ast.expression_boolean_literal(span, false)),
  1012	                Some(arg) => {
  1013	                    let mut arg = arg.take_in(ctx.ast);
  1014	                    Self::minimize_expression_in_boolean_context(&mut arg, ctx);
  1015	                    let arg = ctx.ast.expression_unary(span, UnaryOperator::LogicalNot, arg);
  1016	                    Some(Self::minimize_not(span, arg, ctx))
  1017	                }
  1018	            },
  1019	            "String" => {
  1020	                match arg {
  1021	                    // `String()` -> `''`
  1022	                    None => Some(ctx.ast.expression_string_literal(span, "", None)),
  1023	                    Some(arg) => arg
  1024	                        .evaluate_value_to_string(ctx)
  1025	                        .filter(|_| !arg.may_have_side_effects(ctx))
  1026	                        .map(|s| ctx.value_to_expr(e.span, ConstantValue::String(s))),
  1027	                }
  1028	            }
  1029	            "Number" => Some(ctx.ast.expression_numeric_literal(
  1030	                span,
  1031	                match arg {
  1032	                    None => 0.0,
  1033	                    Some(arg) => match arg.to_number(ctx) {
  1034	                        Some(n) => n,
  1035	                        None => return,
  1036	                    },
  1037	                },
  1038	                None,
  1039	                NumberBase::Decimal,
  1040	            )),
  1041	            // `BigInt(1n)` -> `1n`
  1042	            "BigInt" => match arg {
  1043	                None => None,
  1044	                Some(arg) => {
  1045	                    matches!(arg, Expression::BigIntLiteral(_)).then(|| arg.take_in(ctx.ast))
  1046	                }
  1047	            },
  1048	            _ => None,
  1049	        };
  1050	        if let Some(changed) = changed {
  1051	            *expr = changed;
  1052	            ctx.state.changed = true;
  1053	        }
  1054	    }

  1056	    /// Fold `Object` or `Array` constructor
  1057	    fn get_fold_constructor_name(
  1058	        callee: &Expression<'a>,
  1059	        ctx: &TraverseCtx<'a>,
  1060	    ) -> Option<&'a str> {
  1061	        match callee {
  1062	            Expression::StaticMemberExpression(e) => {
  1063	                if !matches!(&e.object, Expression::Identifier(ident) if ident.name == "window") {
  1064	                    return None;
  1065	                }
  1066	                Some(e.property.name.as_str())
  1067	            }
  1068	            Expression::Identifier(ident) => {
  1069	                let name = ident.name.as_str();
  1070	                if !matches!(name, "Object" | "Array") {
  1071	                    return None;
  1072	                }
  1073	                if !ctx.is_global_reference(ident) {
  1074	                    return None;
  1075	                }
  1076	                Some(name)
  1077	            }
  1078	            _ => None,
  1079	        }
  1080	    }
  1081	
  1082	    /// `window.Object()`, `new Object()`, `Object()`  -> `{}`
  1083	    /// `window.Array()`, `new Array()`, `Array()`  -> `[]`
  1084	    pub fn substitute_object_or_array_constructor(
  1085	        expr: &mut Expression<'a>,
  1086	        ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>,
  1087	    ) {
  1088	        let callee = match expr {
  1089	            Expression::NewExpression(e) => &e.callee,
  1090	            Expression::CallExpression(e) => &e.callee,
  1091	            _ => return,
  1092	        };
  1093	        let Some(name) = Self::get_fold_constructor_name(callee, ctx) else { return };
  1094	        let (span, callee, args, is_new_expr) = match expr {
  1095	            Expression::NewExpression(e) => {
  1096	                let NewExpression { span, callee, arguments, .. } = e.as_mut();
  1097	                (span, callee, arguments, true)
  1098	            }
  1099	            Expression::CallExpression(e) => {
  1100	                let CallExpression { span, callee, arguments, .. } = e.as_mut();
  1101	                (span, callee, arguments, false)
  1102	            }
  1103	            _ => return,
  1104	        };
  1105	        match name {
  1106	            "Object" if args.is_empty() => {
  1107	                *expr = ctx.ast.expression_object(*span, ctx.ast.vec());
  1108	                ctx.state.changed = true;
  1109	            }
  1110	            "Array" => {
  1111	                // `new Array` -> `[]`
  1112	                if args.is_empty() {
  1113	                    *expr = ctx.ast.expression_array(*span, ctx.ast.vec());
  1114	                    ctx.state.changed = true;
  1115	                } else if args.len() == 1 {
  1116	                    let Some(arg) = args[0].as_expression_mut() else { return };
  1117	                    // `new Array(0)` -> `[]`
  1118	                    if arg.is_number_0() {
  1119	                        *expr = ctx.ast.expression_array(*span, ctx.ast.vec());
  1120	                        ctx.state.changed = true;
  1121	                    }
  1122	                    // `new Array(8)` -> `Array(8)`
  1123	                    else if let Expression::NumericLiteral(n) = arg {
  1124	                        // new Array(2) -> `[,,]`
  1125	                        // this does not work with IE8 and below
  1126	                        // learned from https://github.com/babel/minify/pull/45
  1127	                        #[expect(clippy::cast_possible_truncation, clippy::cast_sign_loss)]
  1128	                        if n.value.fract() == 0.0 {
  1129	                            let n_int = n.value as usize;
  1130	                            if (1..=6).contains(&n_int) {
  1131	                                let elisions = repeat_with(|| {
  1132	                                    ArrayExpressionElement::Elision(ctx.ast.elision(n.span))
  1133	                                })
  1134	                                .take(n_int);
  1135	                                *expr = ctx
  1136	                                    .ast
  1137	                                    .expression_array(*span, ctx.ast.vec_from_iter(elisions));
  1138	                                ctx.state.changed = true;
  1139	                                return;
  1140	                            }
  1141	                        }
  1142	                        if is_new_expr {
  1143	                            let callee = callee.take_in(ctx.ast);
  1144	                            let args = args.take_in(ctx.ast);
  1145	                            *expr = ctx.ast.expression_call(*span, callee, NONE, args, false);
  1146	                            ctx.state.changed = true;
  1147	                        }
  1148	                    }
  1149	                    // `new Array(literal)` -> `[literal]`
  1150	                    else if arg.is_literal() || matches!(arg, Expression::ArrayExpression(_)) {

    15	/// Constant Folding
    16	///
    17	/// <https://github.com/google/closure-compiler/blob/v20240609/src/com/google/javascript/jscomp/PeepholeFoldConstants.java>
    18	impl<'a> PeepholeOptimizations {
    19	    #[expect(clippy::float_cmp)]
    20	    pub fn fold_unary_expr(expr: &mut Expression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
    21	        let Expression::UnaryExpression(e) = expr else { return };
    22	        match e.operator {
    23	            // Do not fold `void 0` back to `undefined`.
    24	            UnaryOperator::Void if e.argument.is_number_0() => {}
    25	            // Do not fold `true` and `false` back to `!0` and `!1`
    26	            UnaryOperator::LogicalNot if matches!(&e.argument, Expression::NumericLiteral(lit) if lit.value == 0.0 || lit.value == 1.0) =>
    27	                {}
    28	            // Do not fold big int.
    29	            UnaryOperator::UnaryNegation if e.argument.is_big_int_literal() => {}
    30	            _ if e.may_have_side_effects(ctx) => {}
    31	            _ => {
    32	                if let Some(changed) = e.evaluate_value(ctx).map(|v| ctx.value_to_expr(e.span, v)) {
    33	                    *expr = changed;
    34	                    ctx.state.changed = true;
    35	                }
    36	            }
    37	        }
    38	    }
    39	
    40	    pub fn fold_static_member_expr(expr: &mut Expression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
    41	        let Expression::StaticMemberExpression(e) = expr else { return };
    42	        // TODO: tryFoldObjectPropAccess(n, left, name)
    43	        if e.object.may_have_side_effects(ctx) {
    44	            return;
    45	        }
    46	        if let Some(changed) = e.evaluate_value(ctx).map(|value| ctx.value_to_expr(e.span, value)) {
    47	            *expr = changed;
    48	            ctx.state.changed = true;
    49	        }
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    pub fn fold_computed_member_expr(expr: &mut Expression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
    53	        let Expression::ComputedMemberExpression(e) = expr else { return };
    54	        // TODO: tryFoldObjectPropAccess(n, left, name)
    55	        if e.object.may_have_side_effects(ctx) || e.expression.may_have_side_effects(ctx) {
    56	            return;
    57	        }
    58	        if let Some(changed) = e.evaluate_value(ctx).map(|value| ctx.value_to_expr(e.span, value)) {
    59	            *expr = changed;
    60	            ctx.state.changed = true;
    61	        }
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    pub fn fold_logical_expr(expr: &mut Expression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
    65	        let Expression::LogicalExpression(e) = expr else { return };
    66	        if let Some(changed) = match e.operator {
    67	            LogicalOperator::And | LogicalOperator::Or => Self::try_fold_and_or(e, ctx),
    68	            LogicalOperator::Coalesce => Self::try_fold_coalesce(e, ctx),
    69	        } {
    70	            *expr = changed;
    71	            ctx.state.changed = true;
    72	        }
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    pub fn fold_chain_expr(expr: &mut Expression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
    76	        let Expression::ChainExpression(e) = expr else { return };
    77	        let left_expr = match &e.expression {
    78	            match_member_expression!(ChainElement) => {
    79	                let member_expr = e.expression.to_member_expression();
    80	                if !member_expr.optional() {
    81	                    return;
    82	                }
    83	                member_expr.object()
    84	            }
    85	            ChainElement::CallExpression(call_expr) => {
    86	                if !call_expr.optional {
    87	                    return;
    88	                }
    89	                &call_expr.callee
    90	            }
    91	            ChainElement::TSNonNullExpression(_) => return,
    92	        };
    93	        let ty = left_expr.value_type(ctx);
    94	        if let Some(changed) = (ty.is_null() || ty.is_undefined())
    95	            .then(|| ctx.value_to_expr(e.span, ConstantValue::Undefined))
    96	        {
    97	            *expr = changed;
    98	            ctx.state.changed = true;
    99	        }
   100	    }
   101	
   102	    /// Try to fold a AND / OR node.
   103	    ///
   104	    /// port from [closure-compiler](https://github.com/google/closure-compiler/blob/09094b551915a6487a980a783831cba58b5739d1/src/com/google/javascript/jscomp/PeepholeFoldConstants.java#L587)
   105	    pub fn try_fold_and_or(
   106	        logical_expr: &mut LogicalExpression<'a>,
   107	        ctx: &TraverseCtx<'a>,
   108	    ) -> Option<Expression<'a>> {
   109	        let op = logical_expr.operator;
   110	        debug_assert!(matches!(op, LogicalOperator::And | LogicalOperator::Or));
   111	
   112	        let left = &logical_expr.left;
   113	        let left_val = left.evaluate_value_to_boolean(ctx);
   114	
   115	        if let Some(lval) = left_val {
   116	            // (TRUE || x) => TRUE (also, (3 || x) => 3)
   117	            // (FALSE && x) => FALSE
   118	            if if lval { op.is_or() } else { op.is_and() } {
   119	                return Some(logical_expr.left.take_in(ctx.ast));
   120	            } else if !left.may_have_side_effects(ctx) {
   121	                let should_keep_indirect_access =
   122	                    Self::should_keep_indirect_access(&logical_expr.right, ctx);
   123	                // (true && o.f) => (0, o.f)
   124	                if should_keep_indirect_access {
   125	                    return Some(ctx.ast.expression_sequence(
   126	                        logical_expr.span,
   127	                        ctx.ast.vec_from_array([
   128	                            ctx.ast.expression_numeric_literal(
   129	                                logical_expr.left.span(),
   130	                                0.0,
   131	                                None,
   132	                                NumberBase::Decimal,
   133	                            ),
   134	                            logical_expr.right.take_in(ctx.ast),
   135	                        ]),
   136	                    ));
   137	                }
   138	                // (FALSE || x) => x
   139	                // (TRUE && x) => x
   140	                return Some(logical_expr.right.take_in(ctx.ast));
   141	            }
   142	            // Left side may have side effects, but we know its boolean value.
   143	            // e.g. true_with_sideeffects || foo() => true_with_sideeffects, foo()
   144	            // or: false_with_sideeffects && foo() => false_with_sideeffects, foo()
   145	            let left = logical_expr.left.take_in(ctx.ast);
   146	            let right = logical_expr.right.take_in(ctx.ast);
   147	            let vec = ctx.ast.vec_from_array([left, right]);
   148	            let sequence_expr = ctx.ast.expression_sequence(logical_expr.span, vec);
   149	            return Some(sequence_expr);
   150	        } else if let Expression::LogicalExpression(left_child) = &mut logical_expr.left
   151	            && left_child.operator == logical_expr.operator
   152	        {
   153	            let left_child_right_boolean = left_child.right.evaluate_value_to_boolean(ctx);
   154	            let left_child_op = left_child.operator;
   155	            if let Some(right_boolean) = left_child_right_boolean
   156	                && !left_child.right.may_have_side_effects(ctx)
   157	            {
   158	                // a || false || b => a || b
   159	                // a && true && b => a && b
   160	                if !right_boolean && left_child_op.is_or()
   161	                    || right_boolean && left_child_op.is_and()
   162	                {
   163	                    let left = left_child.left.take_in(ctx.ast);
   164	                    let right = logical_expr.right.take_in(ctx.ast);
   165	                    let logic_expr =
   166	                        ctx.ast.expression_logical(logical_expr.span, left, left_child_op, right);
   167	                    return Some(logic_expr);
   168	                }
   169	            }
   170	        }
   171	        None
   172	    }
   173	
   174	    /// Try to fold a nullish coalesce `foo ?? bar`.
   175	    pub fn try_fold_coalesce(
   176	        logical_expr: &mut LogicalExpression<'a>,
   177	        ctx: &TraverseCtx<'a>,
   178	    ) -> Option<Expression<'a>> {
   179	        debug_assert_eq!(logical_expr.operator, LogicalOperator::Coalesce);
   180	        let left = &logical_expr.left;
   181	        let left_val = left.value_type(ctx);
   182	        match left_val {
   183	            ValueType::Null | ValueType::Undefined => {
   184	                Some(if left.may_have_side_effects(ctx) {
   185	                    // e.g. `(a(), null) ?? 1` => `(a(), null, 1)`
   186	                    let expressions = ctx.ast.vec_from_array([
   187	                        logical_expr.left.take_in(ctx.ast),
   188	                        logical_expr.right.take_in(ctx.ast),
   189	                    ]);
   190	                    ctx.ast.expression_sequence(logical_expr.span, expressions)
   191	                } else {
   192	                    let should_keep_indirect_access =
   193	                        Self::should_keep_indirect_access(&logical_expr.right, ctx);
   194	                    // (null ?? o.f) => (0, o.f)
   195	                    if should_keep_indirect_access {
   196	                        return Some(ctx.ast.expression_sequence(
   197	                            logical_expr.span,
   198	                            ctx.ast.vec_from_array([
   199	                                ctx.ast.expression_numeric_literal(
   200	                                    logical_expr.left.span(),
   201	                                    0.0,
   202	                                    None,
   203	                                    NumberBase::Decimal,
   204	                                ),
   205	                                logical_expr.right.take_in(ctx.ast),
   206	                            ]),
   207	                        ));
   208	                    }
   209	                    // nullish condition => this expression evaluates to the right side.
   210	                    logical_expr.right.take_in(ctx.ast)
   211	                })
   212	            }
   213	            ValueType::Number
   214	            | ValueType::BigInt
   215	            | ValueType::String
   216	            | ValueType::Boolean
   217	            | ValueType::Object => {
   218	                let should_keep_indirect_access =
   219	                    Self::should_keep_indirect_access(&logical_expr.left, ctx);
   220	                // (o.f ?? something) => (0, o.f)
   221	                if should_keep_indirect_access {
   222	                    return Some(ctx.ast.expression_sequence(
   223	                        logical_expr.span,
   224	                        ctx.ast.vec_from_array([
   225	                            ctx.ast.expression_numeric_literal(
   226	                                logical_expr.right.span(),
   227	                                0.0,
   228	                                None,
   229	                                NumberBase::Decimal,
   230	                            ),
   231	                            logical_expr.left.take_in(ctx.ast),
   232	                        ]),
   233	                    ));
   234	                }
   235	                // non-nullish condition => this expression evaluates to the left side.
   236	                Some(logical_expr.left.take_in(ctx.ast))
   237	            }
   238	            ValueType::Undetermined => None,
   239	        }
   240	    }
   241	
   242	    fn extract_numeric_values(e: &BinaryExpression<'a>) -> Option<(f64, f64)> {
   243	        if let (Expression::NumericLiteral(left), Expression::NumericLiteral(right)) =
   244	            (&e.left, &e.right)
   245	        {
   246	            return Some((left.value, right.value));
   247	        }
   248	        None
   249	    }
   250	
   251	    #[expect(clippy::cast_possible_truncation, clippy::cast_sign_loss)]
   252	    pub fn fold_binary_expr(expr: &mut Expression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   253	        let Expression::BinaryExpression(e) = expr else { return };
   254	        // TODO: tryReduceOperandsForOp
   255	
   256	        // https://github.com/evanw/esbuild/blob/v0.24.2/internal/js_ast/js_ast_helpers.go#L1136
   257	        // https://github.com/evanw/esbuild/blob/v0.24.2/internal/js_ast/js_ast_helpers.go#L1222
   258	        let span = e.span;
   259	        let changed = match e.operator {
   260	            BinaryOperator::Equality
   261	            | BinaryOperator::Inequality
   262	            | BinaryOperator::StrictEquality
   263	            | BinaryOperator::StrictInequality
   264	            | BinaryOperator::LessThan
   265	            | BinaryOperator::GreaterThan
   266	            | BinaryOperator::LessEqualThan
   267	            | BinaryOperator::GreaterEqualThan
   268	            | BinaryOperator::ShiftRight
   269	            | BinaryOperator::Instanceof => ctx.eval_binary(e),
   270	            BinaryOperator::BitwiseAnd | BinaryOperator::BitwiseOR | BinaryOperator::BitwiseXOR => {
   271	                ctx.eval_binary(e).or_else(|| Self::try_fold_left_child_op(e, ctx))
   272	            }
   273	            BinaryOperator::Addition => Self::try_fold_add(e, ctx),
   274	            BinaryOperator::Subtraction => {
   275	                // Subtraction of small-ish integers can definitely be folded without issues
   276	                Self::extract_numeric_values(e)
   277	                    .filter(|(left, right)| {
   278	                        left.is_nan()
   279	                            || left.is_finite()
   280	                            || right.is_nan()
   281	                            || right.is_finite()
   282	                            || (left.fract() == 0.0
   283	                                && right.fract() == 0.0
   284	                                && (left.abs() as usize) <= 0xFFFF_FFFF
   285	                                && (right.abs() as usize) <= 0xFFFF_FFFF)
   286	                    })
   287	                    .and_then(|_| ctx.eval_binary(e))
   288	            }
   289	            BinaryOperator::Multiplication
   290	            | BinaryOperator::Exponential
   291	            | BinaryOperator::Remainder => Self::extract_numeric_values(e)
   292	                .filter(|(left, right)| {
   293	                    *left == 0.0
   294	                        || left.is_nan()
   295	                        || left.is_infinite()
   296	                        || *right == 0.0
   297	                        || right.is_nan()
   298	                        || right.is_infinite()
   299	                        // Small number multiplication.
   300	                        || (e.operator == BinaryOperator::Multiplication
   301	                            && left.abs() <= 255.0
   302	                            && left.fract() == 0.0
   303	                            && right.abs() <= 255.0
   304	                            && right.fract() == 0.0)
   305	                })
   306	                .and_then(|_| ctx.eval_binary(e)),
   307	            BinaryOperator::Division => Self::extract_numeric_values(e)
   308	                .filter(|(_, right)| *right == 0.0 || right.is_nan() || right.is_infinite())
   309	                .and_then(|_| ctx.eval_binary(e)),
   310	            BinaryOperator::ShiftLeft => {
   311	                Self::extract_numeric_values(e).and_then(|(left, right)| {
   312	                    let result = e.evaluate_value(ctx)?.into_number()?;
   313	                    let left_len = Self::approximate_printed_int_char_count(left);
   314	                    let right_len = Self::approximate_printed_int_char_count(right);
   315	                    let result_len = Self::approximate_printed_int_char_count(result);
   316	                    (result_len <= left_len + 2 + right_len)
   317	                        .then(|| ctx.value_to_expr(span, ConstantValue::Number(result)))
   318	                })
   319	            }
   320	            BinaryOperator::ShiftRightZeroFill => {
   321	                Self::extract_numeric_values(e).and_then(|(left, right)| {
   322	                    let result = e.evaluate_value(ctx)?.into_number()?;
   323	                    let left_len = Self::approximate_printed_int_char_count(left);
   324	                    let right_len = Self::approximate_printed_int_char_count(right);
   325	                    let result_len = Self::approximate_printed_int_char_count(result);
   326	                    (result_len <= left_len + 3 + right_len)
   327	                        .then(|| ctx.value_to_expr(span, ConstantValue::Number(result)))
   328	                })
   329	            }
   330	            BinaryOperator::In => None,
   331	        };
   332	        if let Some(changed) = changed {
   333	            *expr = changed;
   334	            ctx.state.changed = true;
   335	        }
   336	    }
   337	
   338	    // https://github.com/evanw/esbuild/blob/v0.24.2/internal/js_ast/js_ast_helpers.go#L1128
   339	    #[expect(clippy::cast_possible_truncation, clippy::cast_sign_loss)]
   340	    #[must_use]
   341	    fn approximate_printed_int_char_count(value: f64) -> usize {
   342	        let mut count = if value.is_infinite() {
   343	            "Infinity".len()
   344	        } else if value.is_nan() {
   345	            "NaN".len()
   346	        } else {
   347	            1 + 0.max(value.abs().log10().floor() as usize)
   348	        };
   349	        if value.is_sign_negative() {
   350	            count += 1;
   351	        }
   352	        count
   353	    }

   625	    pub fn fold_object_exp(e: &mut ObjectExpression<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   626	        fn should_fold_spread_element<'a>(e: &Expression<'a>, ctx: &TraverseCtx<'a>) -> bool {
   627	            match e {
   628	                Expression::ArrayExpression(o) if o.elements.is_empty() => true,
   629	                Expression::ArrowFunctionExpression(_) | Expression::FunctionExpression(_) => true,
   630	                e if e.is_literal() && !e.is_string_literal() => true,
   631	                e if e.evaluate_value(ctx).is_some_and(|v| !v.is_string())
   632	                    && !e.may_have_side_effects(ctx) =>
   633	                {
   634	                    true
   635	                }
   636	                _ => false,
   637	            }
   638	        }
   639	        let (new_size, should_fold) =
   640	            e.properties.iter().fold((0, false), |(new_size, should_fold), p| {
   641	                let ObjectPropertyKind::SpreadProperty(spread_element) = p else {
   642	                    return (new_size + 1, should_fold);
   643	                };
   644	                match &spread_element.argument {
   645	                    Expression::ObjectExpression(o)
   646	                        if Self::is_spread_inlineable_object_literal(o, ctx) =>
   647	                    {
   648	                        (new_size + o.properties.len(), true)
   649	                    }
   650	                    e if should_fold_spread_element(e, ctx) => (new_size, true),
   651	                    _ => (new_size + 1, should_fold),
   652	                }
   653	            });
   654	        if !should_fold {
   655	            return;
   656	        }
   657	
   658	        let mut new_properties = ctx.ast.vec_with_capacity::<ObjectPropertyKind>(new_size);
   659	        for p in e.properties.drain(..) {
   660	            if let ObjectPropertyKind::SpreadProperty(mut spread_element) = p {
   661	                let e = &mut spread_element.argument;
   662	                if ctx.is_expression_undefined(e) {
   663	                    continue;
   664	                }
   665	                match e {
   666	                    Expression::ObjectExpression(o)
   667	                        if Self::is_spread_inlineable_object_literal(o, ctx) =>
   668	                    {
   669	                        new_properties.extend(o.properties.drain(..).filter(|prop| {
   670	                            match prop {
   671	                                ObjectPropertyKind::SpreadProperty(_) => true,
   672	                                ObjectPropertyKind::ObjectProperty(p) => {
   673	                                    // non-computed __proto__ property sets the prototype of the object instead
   674	                                    p.computed
   675	                                        || p.method
   676	                                        || !p.key.is_specific_static_name("__proto__")
   677	                                }
   678	                            }
   679	                        }));
   680	                    }
   681	                    e if should_fold_spread_element(e, ctx) => {
   682	                        // skip
   683	                    }
   684	                    _ => {
   685	                        new_properties.push(ObjectPropertyKind::SpreadProperty(spread_element));
   686	                    }
   687	                }
   688	            } else {
   689	                new_properties.push(p);
   690	            }
   691	        }
   692	
   693	        e.properties = new_properties;
   694	        ctx.state.changed = true;
   695	    }
   696	
   697	    fn is_spread_inlineable_object_literal(
   698	        e: &ObjectExpression<'a>,
   699	        ctx: &TraverseCtx<'a>,
   700	    ) -> bool {
   701	        e.properties.iter().all(|p| match p {
   702	            ObjectPropertyKind::SpreadProperty(_) => true,
   703	            ObjectPropertyKind::ObjectProperty(p) => {
   704	                // getters are evaluated when spreading
   705	                matches!(p.kind, PropertyKind::Init)
   706	                    && (
   707	                        // non-computed __proto__ property sets the prototype of the object instead
   708	                        p.computed
   709	                            || p.method
   710	                            || !p.key.is_specific_static_name("__proto__")
   711	                            || !p.value.may_have_side_effects(ctx)
   712	                    )
   713	            }
   714	        })
   715	    }

   717	    /// Inline constant values in template literals
   718	    ///
   719	    /// - `foo${1}bar${i}` => `foo1bar${i}`
   720	    pub fn inline_template_literal(t: &mut TemplateLiteral<'a>, ctx: &mut TraverseCtx<'a>) {
   721	        let has_expr_to_inline = t
   722	            .expressions
   723	            .iter()
   724	            .any(|expr| !expr.may_have_side_effects(ctx) && expr.to_js_string(ctx).is_some());
   725	        if !has_expr_to_inline {
   726	            return;
   727	        }
   728	
   729	        let mut inline_exprs = Vec::with_capacity(t.expressions.len());
   730	        let new_exprs =
   731	            ctx.ast.vec_from_iter(t.expressions.drain(..).enumerate().filter_map(|(idx, expr)| {
   732	                if expr.may_have_side_effects(ctx) {
   733	                    Some(expr)
   734	                } else if let Some(str) = expr.to_js_string(ctx) {
   735	                    inline_exprs.push((idx, str));
   736	                    None
   737	                } else {
   738	                    Some(expr)
   739	                }
   740	            }));
   741	        t.expressions = new_exprs;
   742	
   743	        // inline the extracted inline-able expressions into quasis
   744	        // "current_quasis + extracted_value + next_quasis"
   745	        for (i, (idx, str)) in inline_exprs.into_iter().enumerate() {
   746	            let idx = idx - i;
   747	            let next_quasi = (idx + 1 < t.quasis.len()).then(|| t.quasis.remove(idx + 1));
   748	            let quasi = &mut t.quasis[idx];
   749	            let escaped = Self::escape_string_for_template_literal(&str);
   750	            let next_raw = next_quasi.as_ref().map(|q| q.value.raw.as_str()).unwrap_or_default();

    20	    ///
    21	    /// See also
    22	    ///
    23	    /// ## Statement Fusion
    24	    /// <https://github.com/google/closure-compiler/blob/v20240609/src/com/google/javascript/jscomp/StatementFusion.java>
    25	    ///
    26	    /// ## Collapse variable declarations
    27	    /// `var a; var b = 1; var c = 2` => `var a, b = 1; c = 2`
    28	    /// <https://github.com/google/closure-compiler/blob/v20240609/src/com/google/javascript/jscomp/CollapseVariableDeclarations.java>
    29	    ///
    30	    /// ## Collapse into for statements:
    31	    /// `var a = 0; for(;a<0;a++) {}` => `for(var a = 0;a<0;a++) {}`
    32	    /// <https://github.com/google/closure-compiler/blob/v20240609/src/com/google/javascript/jscomp/Denormalize.java>
    33	    ///
